# Graph Report - autonomous-ai-agency  (2026-07-23)

## Corpus Check
- 1267 files · ~1,728,273 words
- Verdict: corpus is large enough that graph structure adds value.

## Summary
- 23004 nodes · 45755 edges · 1090 communities (981 shown, 109 thin omitted)
- Extraction: 87% EXTRACTED · 13% INFERRED · 0% AMBIGUOUS · INFERRED: 6024 edges (avg confidence: 0.54)
- Token cost: 0 input · 0 output

## Graph Freshness
- Built from commit: `84f65dc3`
- Run `git rev-parse HEAD` and compare to check if the graph is stale.
- Run `graphify update .` after code changes (no API cost).
